for tigers in $(seq 0 20 1000); do
  for goats in $(seq 0 20 1000); do
    echo -n "goats=$goats tigers=$tigers  "
    prism model.prism m.props -sim -simsamples 100 -const init_tigers=$tigers,init_goats=$goats | \
      grep "Result"
  done
done

P=? [ F<=100 (tigers = 0) ]
